## Idea

A map `f : A → B` is **surjective** if all of its
[fibers](foundation-core.fibers-of-maps.md) are
[inhabited](foundation.inhabited-types.md).

## Definition

## Properties

### Any equivalence is surjective

### The dependent universal property of surjective maps

<pre class="Agda"><a id="9491" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="9498" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9498" class="Module">_</a>

  <a id="9567" class="Keyword">where</a>

    <a id="14946" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10654" class="Function">dependent-universal-property-surjection-is-surjectiveᵉ</a> <a id="15001" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14926" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="15004" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14929" class="Bound">is-surj-fᵉ</a>
</pre>
### A map that is both surjective and an embedding is an equivalence

### The composite of a surjective map before an equivalence is surjective

    <a id="19008" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#18446" class="Function">is-surjective-right-map-triangleᵉ</a> <a id="19042" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19043" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#18995" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="19046" href="foundation-core.function-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#476" class="Function Operator">∘ᵉ</a> <a id="19049" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#18999" class="Bound">hᵉ</a><a id="19051" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19053" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#18995" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="19056" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#18999" class="Bound">hᵉ</a> <a id="19059" href="foundation-core.homotopies%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3017" class="Function">refl-htpyᵉ</a>

### Precomposing functions into a family of `k+1`-types by a surjective map is a `k`-truncated map

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-trunc-map-precomp-Π-is-surjectiveᵉ"></a><a id="20230" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20230" class="Function">is-trunc-map-precomp-Π-is-surjectiveᵉ</a> <a id="20268" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="20272" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20273" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20273" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="20277" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20277" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a> <a id="20281" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20281" class="Bound">l3ᵉ</a> <a id="20285" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20287" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="20292" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20294" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20295" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20295" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="20298" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20300" href="foundation-core.truncation-levels%25E1%25B5%2589.html#523" class="Datatype">𝕋ᵉ</a><a id="20302" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20304" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="20308" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20309" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20309" class="Bound">Aᵉ</a> <a id="20312" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20314" href="Agda.Primitive.html#429" class="Primitive">UUᵉ</a> <a id="20318" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20273" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a><a id="20321" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20323" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20324" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20324" class="Bound">Bᵉ</a> <a id="20327" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20329" href="Agda.Primitive.html#429" class="Primitive">UUᵉ</a> <a id="20333" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20277" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a><a id="20336" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20338" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20339" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20339" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="20342" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20344" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20309" class="Bound">Aᵉ</a> <a id="20347" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20349" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20324" class="Bound">Bᵉ</a><a id="20351" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20353" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20355" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2409" class="Function">is-surjectiveᵉ</a> <a id="20370" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20339" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="20373" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="20377" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20378" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20378" class="Bound">Pᵉ</a> <a id="20381" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20383" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20324" class="Bound">Bᵉ</a> <a id="20386" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20388" href="foundation-core.truncated-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1597" class="Function">Truncated-Typeᵉ</a> <a id="20404" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20281" class="Bound">l3ᵉ</a> <a id="20408" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20409" href="foundation-core.truncation-levels%25E1%25B5%2589.html#564" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-𝕋ᵉ</a> <a id="20417" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20295" class="Bound">kᵉ</a><a id="20419" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="20422" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="20426" href="foundation-core.truncated-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#944" class="Function">is-trunc-mapᵉ</a> <a id="20440" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20295" class="Bound">kᵉ</a> <a id="20443" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20444" href="foundation-core.precomposition-dependent-functions%25E1%25B5%2589.html#765" class="Function">precomp-Πᵉ</a> <a id="20455" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20339" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="20458" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="20461" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20461" class="Bound">bᵉ</a> <a id="20464" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20466" href="foundation-core.truncated-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1746" class="Function">type-Truncated-Typeᵉ</a> <a id="20487" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20488" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20378" class="Bound">Pᵉ</a> <a id="20491" href="foundation.surjective-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20461" class="Bound">bᵉ</a><a id="20493" class="Symbol">)))</a>

### The type `Surjection-Into-Truncated-Type l2 (succ-𝕋 k) A` is `k`-truncated

This remains to be shown.
[#735](https://github.com/UniMath/agda-unimath/issues/735)

### Postcomposition of extensions along surjective maps by an embedding is an equivalence

### The type of surjections `A ↠ B` is equivalent to the type of families `P` of inhabited types over `B` equipped with an equivalence `A ≃ Σ B P`

This remains to be shown.
[#735](https://github.com/UniMath/agda-unimath/issues/735)

## See also

- In
  [Epimorphisms with respect to sets](foundation.epimorphisms-with-respect-to-sets.md)
  we show that a map is surjective if and only if it is an epimorphism with
  respect to sets.
